============================================================
-04- COMMANDS
------------------------------------------------------------

?-Shrap
-------
??? times, use the skill 'Shrapnel'

?-TekBa
-------
??? times, use the skill 'TekBarrier'

BlowHas
-------
Use the combo Blow Fish + Haste2.

ConfPoi
-------
Use the combo Confusion + Pois. Frog.

CyclSaf
-------
Use the combo Cyclonic + Safe.

Golem
-------
Use the skill 'Golem'

R-Bless
-------
Use a random ally beneficial-status skill.

  (2/32 chance each)  Big Guard, Golem, Haste
  (1/32 chance each)  Antdot, Bserk, Carbunkl, Fenrir, Float, ForceField, Harvester, Haste2, Kirin, Kitty, Life 3, Palidor, Phantom, Quick, Regen, Remedy, Rflect, Safe, Shell, Tapir, TekBarrier, Unicorn, Vanish, WallChange, Warp, ZoneSeek

R-Chaos
-------
Use a random skill (including broken and glitchy skills).

R-Miss
-------
Use a random skill with low accuracy.

  (5/16 chance each)  Meteo
  (3/16 chance each)  Schiller
  (1/16 chance each)  Blaster, Confusion, Cyclonic, Disaster, Dread, Stone, Virite, X-Zone

R-Nuke
-------
Use a random non-elemental magic damage skill.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  7-Flush, Bahamut, Blow Fish, Bum Rush, Chocobop, Drain, Empowerer, Flare, Flash, GrandTrain, H-Bomb, Heart Burn, HyperDrive, L.4 Flare, Land Slide, Maduin, Meteo, Meteor, Osmose, Quasar, Rage, Rasp, Retort, Revenge, Shock Wave, Shrapnel, Stone, Stunner, TekMissile, Ultima, Whump, Wombat

R-Wind
-------
Use a random wind-elemental skill.

  (2/8 chance each)  Aero, Air Blade, Wind Slash
  (1/8 chance each)  Gale Cut, Sand Storm

W-Phant
-------
2 times, use the skill 'Phantom'

WallCha
-------
Use the skill 'WallChange'
